msg:A very bad accommodation experience. In short, I will never stay in this hotel again!
We booked 2 executive double rooms. First of all, after entering the room, I found that there was no hot water in the basin faucet in the guest room. I asked about the guest room, and an aunt came and said, "Why does your basin need hot water? There is water in this faucet." This is what a five-star standard waiter said words? I replied: I need hot water to wash up! The aunt called a maintenance man and found that the hot water gate under the basin was closed. I don't know whether it was caused by the previous guest or the hotel's problem.
The second thing is that the shower water is cold. I stayed in this hotel for 4 nights and the temperature of the shower water was very low. The hotel's reply was very speechless and asked us to turn on the hot water for a while, saying that it didn't flow out. Several of us were shivering from the cold after taking a shower. Do we need to turn on the machine for a while before the temperature comes up? Third, there was a power outage. The power went out twice in one night. The first time it was out for more than half an hour, and the second time it was out for 15 minutes. The two rooms of the family were so dark that they could not do anything. I complained the next day, but never apologized. I repeatedly explained that the entire floor was out of power and it was uncontrollable. Do I need your weird excuse? The whole floor is out of power, what does it have to do with me? We have been waiting for such a long time and the child is screaming. Does the hotel understand? The first sentence we expect in response should be: I'm sorry!
Fourth, the guest room is unprofessional. We have two adults and one child. We hope that the guest room can find a small quilt. Answer: "You have to take a look, maybe it's not available anymore." There's nothing wrong with this answer, but you have to get back to us later. If it doesn't, it doesn't exist. There was never a reply. We waited for more than an hour and were still awake at 12 o'clock. We were still waiting with the idea that it might happen! Finally, I couldn't wait any longer, so I called again, and the answer was: I want to take a look. Can't you just answer "no"? The quality of training of this service staff is beyond words.
Finally, the breakfast was of very poor quality, with few items, such as drinks, only iced lemonade. Of course, there was still coffee, plus cold and weak black tea. During the Chinese New Year, there were not enough service staff, the breakfast was poor, and other things were really intolerable!
The photo is the view outside the window, the only bright spot that makes people feel comfortable!
